Map/Summary/PAiur01=艾爾的收復行動開始了。神族淨空了躍傳中繼站，黃金艦隊得以橫掃艾爾的天空。然而亞坦尼斯發現有混源體正在指揮野生蟲族群落，他想起澤拉圖預言過的戰爭，當時的警告言猶在耳，令他憂心忡忡。 /// The reclamation of Aiur has begun. With the warp conduits secured, the Golden Armada now sweeps across the planet's skies. But the discovery of a hybrid commanding the once feral zerg broods leaves Artanis troubled over Zeratul's warnings of the war to come.
Map/Summary/PAiur02=亞蒙控制了亞坦尼斯，在澤拉圖試圖斬斷亞坦尼斯的神經索時殺死了澤拉圖。如今卡拉已被腐化，與卡拉相連的神族全都落入亞蒙的掌控。年輕的大主教沒有時間哀悼好友的逝去，他努力集合剩餘的部隊；同時，殘存的黑暗聖堂武士正在努力拯救更多的同胞。 /// Zeratul is dead, slain by Amon while severing Artanis's nerve cords. But the young Hierarch has much to do before he can grieve for his fallen friend. The Khala is corrupted, binding all those within it to Amon's will. Artanis rallies his remaining forces as the last of the Dark Templar work to free more of their brethren.
Map/Summary/PAiur03=艾爾落入亞蒙的手中。殘存的聖堂武士登上亞頓之矛逃離他們的家園，暫時脫離了亞蒙的魔掌。在失去卡拉和黃金艦隊的情況下，亞坦尼斯必須先尋求老朋友和新盟友的協助，才能再次對抗黑暗主宰。
Map/Summary/PAiur04=了結亞蒙的時刻終於來臨。亞坦尼斯和他的盟友分工合作，破壞了位在艾爾各地的躍傳網路，並成功阻止黃金艦隊到來。但目前所做的只是拖延聯合艦隊的抵達時間而已，他們終究還是得趕在艦隊抵達前，摧毀亞蒙的軀體。 /// The time has come to end Amon once and for all. Working together across all of Aiur, Artanis and his allies have destroyed the planet's warp network and prevented the return of the Golden Armada. But they have only delayed the Great Fleet's arrival, and must use the time they have left to eliminate Amon's host body.
Map/Summary/PAiur05=經過了激烈的戰鬥，亞坦尼斯和他的夥伴趕在亞蒙復活之前摧毀了他的軀體，但他們仍然得把亞蒙困在星鑰石之內，好讓其他聖堂武士有機會脫離卡拉的控制。最終決戰近在眼前，屆時亞蒙會傾盡全力應戰，唯有團結一致，他們才能與之抗衡。 /// After a hard fought battle, Artanis and his allies destroyed Amon's host body just as it came to life. But they must still imprison Amon within the Keystone long enough for the rest of the Templar to sever themselves from the Khala. The final confrontation lies ahead, and Amon will bring all of his might down upon them. Only in unity can they prevail.
Map/Summary/PAiur06=亞蒙被擊敗後，被放逐回虛空之中。雖然神族失去了卡拉，但他們即將開創嶄新的黃金時代。由於各位戰士與英雄們勇敢無畏的行為，終於迎來和平的一線曙光。然而亞蒙並未真正死去，眼前的要務仍然未解。<n/><n/>在《星海爭霸II》三部曲的終章「深入虛空」中見證這場史詩之戰的結局。 /// Amon has been defeated and banished back into the Void. Though the Khala is no more, the protoss stand on the cusp of a new golden age. Thanks to the efforts and sacrifices of brave warriors and heroes, peace can once again be glimpsed upon the horizon. But one final task remains if Amon is to be truly destroyed.<n/><n/>Experience the epic conclusion with Into the Void, the final chapter in the StarCraft II trilogy.
Map/Summary/PKorhal01=亞坦尼斯和雷諾聯手阻止天盾太空站免於墜毀，化解了克哈星的危機。莫比斯部隊的威脅消失後，亞坦尼斯把目標轉回當初他前往自治聯盟的理由：取得星鑰石和追尋澤拉圖的預言。 /// Sky Shield's catastrophic descent into Korhal's atmosphere has been prevented, thanks to the combined efforts of Artanis and Raynor. With the threat of Moebius Corps forestalled, Artanis turns his attention to the reason for his journey into Dominion space: acquiring the Keystone and pursuing Zeratul's prophecies.
Map/Summary/PKorhal02=星鑰石終於到手了，但人類在這場爭奪星鑰石之戰中傷亡慘重。亞蒙軍隊所到之處對自治聯盟造成難以抹滅的傷害，留下遍地的傷亡與破壞。雷諾與亞坦尼斯現在告別彼此，兩人都決心為保衛自己同胞的未來而奮戰。 /// The Keystone has been secured, though the terrans have suffered enormous casualties in the process. Even now, Amon's forces cut a swath through Dominion space, leaving death and destruction in their wake. Raynor and Artanis now go their separate ways, each of them determined to fight for the survival of their people.
Map/Summary/PMoebius01=凱拉克在亞坦尼斯的戰士防衛亞頓之矛時，不畏艱難，成功摧毀了亞蒙最後一座混源體繁殖設施。儘管凱拉克是個未經戰鬥訓練的卡萊相位工匠，他的英勇壯舉足以與任何聖堂武士媲美。
Map/Summary/PPurifier01=儘管亞拉瑞克和塔達力姆奮力阻撓，亞坦尼斯仍然成功從葛拉西斯的卡萊設施中取得了淨化者武器試驗品。凱拉克深信，這個新科技會在他們和亞蒙的戰爭中派上用場。 /// Despite the efforts of Alarak and the Tal'darim, Artanis has retrieved a cache of experimental Purifier weaponry from a Khalai facility on Glacius. Karax is confident that this new technology will prove invaluable in the war against Amon.
Map/Summary/PPurifier02=亞坦尼斯的軍隊在安迪昂的蟲族感染中殺出一條血路，成功解除賽博洛斯數百年來的靜滯狀態。現在，他們可以喚醒戰艦上的古老淨化者了。即便淨化者對首生者滿懷敵意，亞坦尼斯仍堅信，他們會幫助他對抗亞蒙。 /// Artanis's forces have cleared a path through the zerg infestation on Endion and released Cybros from its centuries in stasis. Now the ancient Purifiers aboard the warship can be reawakened. Despite their hostility toward the Firstborn, Artanis is confident he can secure their support in the war against Amon.
Map/Summary/PPurifier03=淨化者再度甦醒了。在執行官庫勒瑞安的指揮下，他們從蟲族的手中淨化了賽博洛斯，收復他們的家園。他們會是強大的盟友，但在此之前，亞坦尼斯必須彌補過去的錯誤，說服淨化者放下長久以來的敵意，別再憎恨他們的神族創造者。 /// The Purifiers are awake once again. Under the command of Executor Clolarion, they have cleansed Cybros of the zerg and reclaimed it as their home. They could prove to be powerful allies... but first, Artanis must make amends for the past and convince them to set aside their age-old enmity toward their protoss creators.
Map/Summary/PShakuras01=亞蒙的混源體和蟲族在夏庫拉斯肆虐，在這場攻擊中，成千上萬的尼拉辛姆被屠殺。倖存者從地表撤離，跟隨大族長芙菈森加入亞坦尼斯一同作戰。黑暗聖堂武士是強而有力的盟友，然而在亞蒙無情的進攻之下，夏庫拉斯很可能會就此落入亞蒙手中。 /// Shakuras is overrun with Amon's hybrid and zerg, and countless Nerazim were slaughtered in the attack. Those that survive have been evacuated from the planet's surface and now follow Matriarch Vorazun alongside Artanis. The Dark Templar make for strong allies, but Shakuras may be lost to Amon's unrelenting advance.
Map/Summary/PShakuras02=為了不讓亞蒙奪走夏庫拉斯，這顆星球在巨大的爆炸中化為塵埃。神族已無家可歸，流離失所的族人身處亞頓之矛，計畫著反攻敵人的大業。 /// Shakuras is no more, obliterated in a massive explosion to prevent Amon from seizing the planet as his own. The protoss now stand without a home, a vagabond people aboard the Spear of Adun, seeking a way to strike back at their great enemy.
Map/Summary/PTaldarim01=亞拉瑞克以雙方停火為條件，讓亞坦尼斯同意協助他篡奪塔達力姆的領導之位。在亞拉瑞克的堅持下，亞坦尼斯跟瑪拉許大領主的護衛官戰鬥並消滅了他們，然後才發現自己受騙，他們和儀式毫不相干。 /// In exchange for a ceasefire between their people, Artanis has agreed to aid Alarak in usurping the leadership of the Tal'darim. At Alarak's insistence, Artanis eliminated Highlord Ma'lash's guardians... only to learn that he had been deceived, and that the battle had nothing to do with the ritual.
Map/Summary/PTaldarim02=亞拉瑞克殺死瑪拉許，掌控了所有的塔達力姆。他們現在背棄亞蒙，不再與亞坦尼斯的部隊為敵。不過，如果亞坦尼斯能說服亞拉瑞克加入他的陣營，他將是一股強大的助力。 /// Alarak has slain Ma'lash and seized control of the Tal'darim.  They now turn against Amon and no longer present a threat to Artanis's forces. If he can convince Alarak to fight alongside him, however, Artanis stands to gain a powerful new ally.
Map/Summary/PUlnar01=在星鑰石的帶領下，亞頓之矛來到奧納。傳說中，這裡是薩爾納加的家園。亞坦尼斯從塔達力姆手中奪回神殿，打開通往內部的入口。實現澤拉圖最後預言的時刻，終於到來。 /// Led by the Keystone, the Spear of Adun now orbits Ulnar, fabled home of the xel'naga. Artanis has secured the temple from the Tal'darim and unsealed the entrance into the halls below. The time to fulfill Zeratul's final prophecy has come to pass.
Map/Summary/PUlnar02=亞坦尼斯和刀鋒女皇一起解開了薩爾納加創造這一切的目的，並進入他們的沉眠之所。但為時已晚，亞蒙殺了他的同胞，而且正準備進入他自己打造的軀殼，澤拉圖所言的希望似乎已化為烏有。但在希望如此渺茫的這一刻，亞坦尼斯的意志仍堅定不移。 /// Alongside the Queen of Blades, Artanis has uncovered the great purpose of the xel'naga and entered the chamber wherein they slumber. But he is too late. Amon has killed his brethren and is now poised to enter a host body of his own creation. The hope heralded by Zeratul seems lost, but Artanis stands firm against the dying light.
Map/Summary/PUlnar03=亞蒙背叛了塔達力姆，亞拉瑞克在盛怒之下前往通知芙菈森，亞坦尼斯即將有性命危險。芙菈森滿腹懷疑地接受他的幫助，帶領駐守在亞頓之矛的聖堂武士展開大膽的營救行動。此刻無法仰賴澤拉圖的預言來指引神族方向，現在他們得自行摸索找出生路。 /// Incensed by Amon's betrayal of the Tal'darim, Alarak warns Vorazun that Artanis is in danger. After reluctantly accepting his help, Vorazun leads the Templar aboard the Spear of Adun in a daring rescue of their Hierarch. Without Zeratul's prophecies to guide them, the protoss must now chart a new course of action on their own.
Map/Summary/SC2Epilogue01=凱莉根、雷諾和亞坦尼斯帶領他們的部隊直入虛空，打算一舉消滅亞蒙。戰況艱辛而激烈，但他們的軍隊成功殺死了那魯，在這個黑暗的世界中攻下一個據點。有個神秘卻充滿善意的聲音呼籲他們採取行動，現在他們開始尋找這個聲音的來源。 /// Kerrigan, Raynor and Artanis lead their forces on an expedition into the Void to end Amon once and for all. The battle has been difficult, but their armies have nonetheless succeeded in killing Narud and establishing a foothold within this dark realm. Now they seek the source of the mysterious yet benevolent voice that called them to action.
Map/Summary/SC2Epilogue02=凱莉根面對天命的時候已到。她在雷諾和亞坦尼斯的協助下，接收了最後一位薩爾納加歐洛斯的原質。凱莉根在繼承了驚人的力量之後，已準備好要終結亞蒙的性命。 /// The time has come for Kerrigan to embrace her destiny. With the help of Raynor and Artanis, she has absorbed the essence of Ouros, last of the xel'naga. With the awesome power she has inherited, she stands ready to end Amon once and for all.
Map/Summary/SC2Epilogue03=歷經千辛萬苦之後，亞蒙終於灰飛煙滅。凱莉根成為薩爾納加，終結了無盡的循環。克普魯星區的居民現在投入全副心力重建家園、休養生息，不枉凱莉根勇敢無私的犧牲。<n/><n/>帝國殞落，星球毀滅，而眾神消亡：勇敢的領袖們歷盡千辛萬苦，帶領部隊獲得勝利，為自己的同胞贏得了自由與和平。《星海爭霸II》的史詩傳奇在此劃下句點，謝謝你的支持。 /// At long last, Amon is no more. Kerrigan has become xel'naga and ended the Infinite Cycle. The denizens of the Koprulu sector now focus on reconstruction and recovery, making the most of Kerrigan's valiant sacrifice.<n/><n/>Empires have fallen, worlds have been shattered, and gods have been slain. Through it all, brave commanders have led their forces to victory and secured peace and freedom for their people. The saga of StarCraft II has ended. Thank you for playing.
